Constants

ICScannerDocumentTypeDefault

Document size types. Corresponds to “ICAP_SUPPORTEDSIZES” used by the Image Catpure scanner modules. Also refer to TWAIN 1.9 Specification, page 9-483. @constant ICScannerDocumentTypeDefault This is the platten size.
